; =============================================
; Epson HX-20 ROM Disassembly (unknown-012905)
; HD6301/HD6303 instruction set
; =============================================

; I/O Register Map:
; $00-$14: HD6301 internal registers
;   $00: P1DDR  $01: P2DDR  $02: PORT1  $03: PORT2
;   $04: P3DDR  $05: P4DDR  $06: PORT3  $07: PORT4
;   $08: TCSR   $09: FRCH   $0A: FRCL   $0B: OCRH
;   $0C: OCRL   $0D: ICRH   $0E: ICRL   $0F: P3CSR
;   $10: RMCR   $11: TRCSR  $12: RDR    $13: TDR
;   $14: RAMCR
; $20: KSC (keyboard scan)  $22: KRTN07  $26: LCD control
; $28: KRTN89  $2A: LCD data  $2C: INT mask
; $40-$7F: MC146818 RTC
;   $4A: RTC_REGA  $4B: RTC_REGB  $4C: RTC_REGC  $4D: RTC_REGD
; $80-$FF: Internal RAM
; $0100-$3FFF: External RAM (16KB)
; $8000-$FFFF: ROM (32KB)
